    class NodePool {
        +apiVersion: string
        +kind: string
        +metadata: object
        +spec: NodePoolSpec
        +status: NodePoolStatus
    }
    class NodePoolSpec {
        +disruption: Disruption
        +limits: object
        +template: NodeClaimTemplate
        +weight: integer
    }
    class Disruption {
        +budgets: Budget[]
        +consolidateAfter: string
        +consolidationPolicy: enum
        +expireAfter: string
    }
    class Budget {
        +duration: string
        +nodes: string
        +schedule: string
    }
    class NodeClaimTemplate {
        +metadata: TemplateMetadata
        +spec: NodeClaimSpec
    }
    class TemplateMetadata {
        +annotations: object
        +labels: object
    }
    class NodeClaimSpec {
        +kubelet: Kubelet
        +nodeClassRef: NodeClassRef
        +requirements: Requirement[]
        +resources: Resources
        +startupTaints: Taint[]
        +taints: Taint[]
    }
    class Kubelet {
        +clusterDNS: string[]
        +cpuCFSQuota: boolean
        +evictionHard: object
        +evictionMaxPodGracePeriod: int32
        +evictionSoft: object
        +evictionSoftGracePeriod: object
        +imageGCHighThresholdPercent: int32
        +imageGCLowThresholdPercent: int32
        +kubeReserved: object
        +maxPods: int32
        +podsPerCore: int32
        +systemReserved: object
    }
    class NodeClassRef {
        +apiVersion: string
        +kind: string
        +name: string
    }
    class Requirement {
        +key: string
        +minValues: integer
        +operator: enum
        +values: string[]
    }
    class Resources {
        +requests: object
    }
    class Taint {
        +effect: enum
        +key: string
        +timeAdded: date-time
        +value: string
    }
    class NodePoolStatus {
        +resources: object
    }

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Created: NodePool Created
    Created --> Configuring: Validate Spec
    Configuring --> Active: Apply Configuration
    Active --> Disrupting: Budget/Policy Triggered
    Disrupting --> ConsolidatingNodes: WhenUnderutilized
    Disrupting --> EmptyingNodes: WhenEmpty
    ConsolidatingNodes --> Active: Consolidation Complete
    EmptyingNodes --> Active: Nodes Terminated
    Active --> Expired: ExpireAfter Reached
    Expired --> Terminating: Remove Nodes
    Terminating --> [*]
    Active --> Active: Monitor Resources
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([NodePool Definition]) --> ValidateSpec{Validate Spec}
    ValidateSpec -->|Invalid| Error([Error])
    ValidateSpec -->|Valid| CheckDisruption{Check Disruption Policy}
    CheckDisruption --> SetBudgets[Set Budget Constraints]
    SetBudgets --> ConfigTemplate[Configure NodeClaim Template]
    ConfigTemplate --> SetMetadata[Set Metadata/Labels]
    SetMetadata --> ConfigKubelet[Configure Kubelet Settings]
    ConfigKubelet --> SetRequirements[Set Node Requirements]
    SetRequirements --> SetTaints[Apply Taints]
    SetTaints --> SetNodeClassRef[Reference NodeClass]
    SetNodeClassRef --> ApplyLimits[Apply Resource Limits]
    ApplyLimits --> SetWeight[Set Scheduling Weight]
    SetWeight --> MonitorNodes[Monitor Node Resources]
    MonitorNodes --> CheckExpiry{Check Expiry}
    CheckExpiry -->|Expired| TerminateNode[Terminate Node]
    CheckExpiry -->|Active| CheckUtilization{Check Utilization}
    CheckUtilization -->|Underutilized| Consolidate[Consolidate Nodes]
    CheckUtilization -->|Empty| Empty[Terminate Empty Nodes]
    CheckUtilization -->|Optimal| MonitorNodes
    Consolidate --> MonitorNodes
    Empty --> MonitorNodes
    TerminateNode --> MonitorNodes
```
